:i $hat$ = :a{
	:i :s{
		:i $desc_id$ = $None$
		:i $frontend_desc$ = %sc(4,"None")
		:i function $disqualify_script$
			:i $ClearPart$$part$ = $hat_logo$
			:i $ClearPart$$part$ = $skater_m_hat_hair$
			:i $ClearPart$$part$ = $skater_f_hat_hair$
		:i endfunction
		:i $lockout_parts$ = :a{$skater_m_hat_hair$$skater_f_hat_hair$:a}
		:i $no_color$
		:i $null_item$
	:i :s}
	:i :s{
		:i $desc_id$ = $Forward Cap$

			:i $ClearPart$$part$ = $skater_m_hair$

		:i endfunction
		:i $supports_logo$
